		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '77a72a7f35d248d642b5726a063f8bcf932e0492') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');

		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '77a72a7f35d248d642b5726a063f8bcf932e0492') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '77a72a7f35d248d642b5726a063f8bcf932e0492') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/000_objects/OIDplusPagePublicObjects.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/000_objects/OIDplusPagePublicObjects.class.php') !== 'd23131ca3e1957ba03d9ac778c96d50de1b3fd34') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/000_objects/OIDplusPagePublicObjects.class.php');
		}
	}
}
